## Feature Hierarchy

Derived concepts shown as top-level features with their composed concepts nested underneath.

### ActionGuideDoc <sub>interface</sub>

> Generate structured action guide documentation by classifying 
 and grouping concept actions , then rendering enriched output .

**Composes**: ActionGuide, EnrichmentRenderer, Grouping
**Required syncs**: grouping-guide-structure, guide-renderer-format

**Surface**:
- `define` &rarr; ActionGuide/define
- `render` &rarr; ActionGuide/render
- `classify` &rarr; Grouping/classify

#### ActionGuide [W]

> Organize concept actions into ordered , annotated workflow 
 sequences for interface targets . The concept owns step 
 ordering ( structural ) and opaque content passthrough for 
 decorations . Each target reads the content keys it 
 understands ( checklists , design principles , anti patterns , 
 validation commands , etc . ) and ignores the rest . New 
 decoration kinds require only a new YAML key and a 
 renderer in the target provider zero concept changes . 
 Renamed from Workflow to avoid collision with 
 suites automation workflow . concept ( FSM with guarded transitions ) . 
 See Architecture doc Section 1.8 .

**State**:
- `workflows: Set<W>`
- `concept: W Ôćĺ String`
- `steps: W Ôćĺ List<{ action: String, title: String, prose: String, order: Int }>`
- `content: W Ôćĺ String`

**Actions**:
- `define(concept: String, steps: List<String>, content: String)` &rarr; ok | invalidAction | emptySteps
- `render(workflow: W, format: String)` &rarr; ok | unknownFormat

#### EnrichmentRenderer [R]

> Render opaque enrichment JSON into formatted output strings 
 using data driven templates . Handlers are declarative each 
 maps an enrichment key to a built in render pattern ( list , 
 checklist , code list , callout , heading body , bad good , etc . ) 
 plus a template config with { { field } } interpolation . Patterns 
 are the small code surface shipped once ; handlers are pure 
 data that can live in YAML manifests . New enrichment kinds 
 need only a YAML entry zero code changes . 
 Renamed from Renderer to avoid collision with 
 suites presentation renderer . concept ( cache aware rendering pipeline ) . 
 See Architecture doc Section 1.8 .

**State**:
- `handlers: Set<R>`
- `key: R Ôćĺ String`
- `format: R Ôćĺ String`
- `order: R Ôćĺ Int`
- `pattern: R Ôćĺ String`
- `template: R Ôćĺ String`

**Actions**:
- `register(key: String, format: String, order: Int, pattern: String, template: String)` &rarr; ok | unknownPattern | invalidTemplate
- `render(content: String, format: String)` &rarr; ok | invalidContent | unknownFormat
- `listHandlers(format: String)` &rarr; ok
- `listPatterns()` &rarr; ok

#### Grouping [G]

> Organize concepts into named groups using structural or 
 behavioral classification strategies for interface generation 
 targets . Structural strategies group by concept identity or 
 suite membership . Behavioral strategies group by dominant action 
 classification ( CRUD role , read write intent , event producing 
 status , or MCP resource type ) .

**State**:
- `groupings: Set<G>`
- `strategy: G Ôćĺ String`
- `itemCount: G Ôćĺ Int`
- `entries: G Ôćĺ List<{ name: String, description: String, members: List<String> }>`

**Actions**:
- `group(items: List<String>, config: String)` &rarr; ok | invalidStrategy | emptyInput
- `classify(actionName: String)` &rarr; ok

### ApiEndpoint <sub>interface</sub>

> Compose interface projection , middleware injection , spec generation , 
 and API surface composition into a complete API endpoint definition .

**Composes**: Projection, Middleware, Spec, ApiSurface
**Required syncs**: projection-middleware-inject, projection-spec-emit, spec-surface-compose

**Surface**:
- `project` &rarr; Projection/project
- `injectMiddleware` &rarr; Middleware/inject
- `emitSpec` &rarr; Spec/emit
- `compose` &rarr; ApiSurface/compose

#### Projection [P]

> Enrich ConceptManifests with interface generation metadata . 
 Reads concept specs ( via ConceptManifest from SchemaGen ) and 
 interface annotations ( from app . interface . yaml ) , produces 
 generation ready projections with resource mappings , trait 
 bindings , cross concept type graphs , and opaque enrichment 
 content . Enrichment is stored as a single JSON string 
 targets interpret keys they recognize ( workflows , 
 annotations , command tree , action mappings ) and ignore the 
 rest . One projection per concept per generation run .

**State**:
- `projections: Set<P>`
- `concept: P Ôćĺ String`
- `kitName: P Ôćĺ String`
- `kitVersion: P Ôćĺ String`
- `conceptManifest: P Ôćĺ String`
- `traits: P Ôćĺ List<{ name: String, scope: String, config: String }>`
- `resourceMapping: P Ôćĺ { path: String, idField: String, actions: List<String> }?`
- `targetOverrides: P Ôćĺ List<{ target: String, config: String }>`
- `shapes: P Ôćĺ List<{ name: String, kind: String, resolved: String }>`
- `crossReferences: P Ôćĺ List<{ from: String, to: String, relation: String }>`
- `content: P Ôćĺ String`

**Actions**:
- `project(manifest: String, annotations: String)` &rarr; ok | annotationError | unresolvedReference | traitConflict
- `validate(projection: P)` &rarr; ok | breakingChange | incompleteAnnotation
- `diff(projection: P, previous: P)` &rarr; ok | incompatible
- `inferResources(projection: P)` &rarr; ok

#### Middleware [M]

> Map abstract interface traits to concrete middleware 
 implementations per target . @ auth ( bearer ) produces 
 Bearer token validation in REST , metadata interceptor 
 in gRPC , env var check in CLI , OAuth flow in MCP . 
 Owns trait definitions , per target implementations , 
 composition ordering , and compatibility rules .

**State**:
- `definitions: Set<M>`
- `name: M Ôćĺ String`
- `scope: M Ôćĺ String`
- `config: M Ôćĺ String`
- `implementations: M Ôćĺ List<{ target: String, code: String, position: String }>`
- `order: M Ôćĺ Int`
- `dependsOn: M Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `incompatibleWith: M Ôćĺ List<String>`

**Actions**:
- `resolve(traits: List<String>, target: String)` &rarr; ok | missingImplementation | incompatibleTraits
- `inject(output: String, middlewares: List<String>, target: String)` &rarr; ok
- `register(trait: String, target: String, implementation: String, position: String)` &rarr; ok | duplicateRegistration

#### Spec [D]

> Coordinate specification document generation . Owns the 
 spec registry , versioning , and cross concept composition 
 ( a single OpenAPI document covers all concepts in a suite ) . 
 Generator talks to Spec , never to format providers directly .

**State**:
- `documents: Set<D>`
- `format: D Ôćĺ String`
- `kitName: D Ôćĺ String`
- `version: D Ôćĺ String`
- `generatedAt: D Ôćĺ DateTime`

#### ApiSurface [S]

> Compose generated interfaces from multiple concepts into 
 a cohesive , unified API surface per target . For REST : a 
 single router with concept namespaced routes . For GraphQL : 
 a merged schema with shared types . For CLI : a command tree 
 with concept subcommands . For MCP : a combined tool set . 
 For SDKs : a single client with concept namespaced methods . 
 Renamed from Surface to avoid collision with 
 concept interface suites surface render surface . concept 
 ( runtime rendering target for DOM , terminal , etc . ) .

**State**:
- `surfaces: Set<S>`
- `suite: S Ôćĺ String`
- `target: S Ôćĺ String`
- `concepts: S Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `entrypoint: S Ôćĺ String`
- `routes: S Ôćĺ List<{ path: String, concept: String, action: String }>?`
- `sharedTypes: S Ôćĺ List<{ name: String, usedBy: List<String> }>?`

**Actions**:
- `compose(suite: String, target: String, outputs: List<String>)` &rarr; ok | conflictingRoutes | cyclicDependency
- `entrypoint(surface: S)` &rarr; ok

### AppShell <sub>ui-app</sub>

#### Navigator [N]

> Manage transitions between abstract destinations and 
 maintain navigation history . Each destination associates 
 a name with a target concept and view configuration . 
 Navigation state is a stack of previously visited 
 destinations supporting back forward traversal .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `destinations: Set<N>`
- `name: N Ôćĺ String`
- `targetConcept: N Ôćĺ String`
- `targetView: N Ôćĺ String`
- `paramsSchema: N Ôćĺ String?`
- `meta: N Ôćĺ String?`
- `current: N Ôćĺ N?`
- `history: N Ôćĺ List<N>`
- `forwardStack: N Ôćĺ List<N>`
- `guards: N Ôćĺ List<String>`

**Actions**:

#### ThemeSystem <sub>ui-theme</sub>

> Unify theme creation , color palettes , typography scales , elevation 
 shadows , motion curves , and design tokens into a cohesive 
 design system with token resolution .

**Composes**: Theme, Palette, Typography, Elevation, Motion, DesignToken
**Required syncs**: theme-palette-bind, theme-typography-bind, theme-elevation-bind, theme-motion-bind, theme-token-resolve

**Surface**:
- `createTheme` &rarr; Theme/create
- `activateTheme` &rarr; Theme/activate
- `defineToken` &rarr; DesignToken/define
- `generatePalette` &rarr; Palette/generate

##### Theme [H]

> Compose tokens into a complete visual language . A Theme is a 
 named collection of token overrides : dark remaps color background 
 from white to gray -900 . Themes are layered : base variants . 
 Multiple variants can be active ( dark compact high contrast ) . 
 Conflicts resolve by specificity then activation order .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `name: H Ôćĺ String`
- `base: H Ôćĺ H?`
- `overrides: H Ôćĺ String`
- `active: H Ôćĺ Bool`
- `priority: H Ôćĺ Int`

**Actions**:
- `create(theme: H, name: String, overrides: String)` &rarr; ok | duplicate
- `extend(theme: H, base: H, overrides: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `activate(theme: H, priority: Int)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `deactivate(theme: H)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `resolve(theme: H)` &rarr; ok | notfound

##### Palette [C]

> Color system with semantic roles and WCAG accessibility enforcement . 
 Generates complete 50 -950 color scales from seed colors using 
 perceptual color space ( OKLCH ) . Every color pair validated against 
 WCAG 2.1 : AA ( 4.5 : 1 normal , 3 : 1 large ) and AAA ( 7 : 1 normal ) .

**State**:
- `name: C Ôćĺ String`
- `hue: C Ôćĺ Float`
- `scale: C Ôćĺ String`
- `role: C Ôćĺ String?`
- `contrastRatio: C Ôćĺ Float?`

**Actions**:
- `generate(palette: C, name: String, seed: String)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `assignRole(palette: C, role: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `checkContrast(foreground: C, background: C)` &rarr; ok | notfound

##### Typography [X]

> Type scale , font stacks , and text styles . Generates harmonious 
 type scale from modular ratio ( default : major third , 1.25 ) . 
 Composes scale sizes with font stacks and weights into named 
 presets : heading -1 , body , caption , label , code .

**State**:
- `name: X Ôćĺ String`
- `kind: X Ôćĺ String`
- `value: X Ôćĺ String`
- `scale: X Ôćĺ String?`

**Actions**:
- `defineScale(typography: X, baseSize: Float, ratio: Float, steps: Int)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `defineFontStack(typography: X, name: String, fonts: String, category: String)` &rarr; ok | duplicate
- `defineStyle(typography: X, name: String, config: String)` &rarr; ok | invalid

##### Elevation [W]

> Shadow and depth system . Numbered scale ( 0 -5 ) : 
 0 = flat , 1 = raised , 2 = floating , 3 = overlay , 
 4 = modal , 5 = top . Each level uses multi layer shadows . 
 Adapts to theme : light uses gray shadows , dark uses 
 darker shadows or ambient glow .

**State**:
- `level: W Ôćĺ Int`
- `shadow: W Ôćĺ String`
- `color: W Ôćĺ String?`

**Actions**:
- `define(elevation: W, level: Int, shadow: String)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `get(elevation: W)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `generateScale(baseColor: String)` &rarr; ok | invalid

##### Motion [O]

> Animation timing , easing , and transitions . All values are 
 named , referenceable , and overridable via themes . Respects 
 prefers reduced motion : all durations collapse to 0 ms .

**State**:

##### DesignToken [T]

> Store design decisions as structured , platform agnostic data . 
 Tokens are the atomic unit of visual design a color value , 
 a spacing size , a font family . They form a three tier 
 hierarchy : primitive ( raw values ) , semantic ( meaning purpose ) , 
 and component ( bound to specific UI elements ) . Follows the 
 W3C Design Tokens Community Group specification ( 2025.10 ) .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `name: T Ôćĺ String`
- `value: T Ôćĺ String`
- `type: T Ôćĺ String`
- `tier: T Ôćĺ String`
- `description: T Ôćĺ String?`
- `reference: T Ôćĺ T?`
- `group: T Ôćĺ String?`

**Actions**:
- `define(token: T, name: String, value: String, type: String, tier: String)` &rarr; ok | duplicate
- `alias(token: T, name: String, reference: T, tier: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound | cycle
- `resolve(token: T)` &rarr; ok | notfound | broken
- `update(token: T, value: String?)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `remove(token: T)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `export(format: String)` &rarr; ok | unsupported

##### Layout [Y]

> Spatial arrangement of components . Describes positioning 
 without specifying CSS or terminal coordinates constraint based 
 descriptions interpreted per Surface . Layouts compose recursively : 
 a page layout contains region layouts containing component layouts .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `name: Y Ôćĺ String`

##### Viewport [V]

> Responsive breakpoint and adaptation . Observes surface dimensions , 
 evaluates breakpoint conditions , produces active breakpoints for 
 Layout and Widget via signals . Defaults : xs ( 0 -479 ) , sm ( 480 -767 ) , 
 md ( 768 -1023 ) , lg ( 1024 -1279 ) , xl ( 1280 ) .

**State**:
- `width: V Ôćĺ Int`
- `height: V Ôćĺ Int`
- `breakpoint: V Ôćĺ String`
- `orientation: V Ôćĺ String`
- `customBreakpoints: V Ôćĺ String?`

**Actions**:
- `observe(viewport: V, width: Int, height: Int)` &rarr; ok
- `setBreakpoints(viewport: V, breakpoints: String)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `getBreakpoint(viewport: V)` &rarr; ok | notfound

### BuildPipeline <sub>framework</sub>

> Compose resource tracking , build caching , generation planning , 
 kind-system classification , and file emission into a complete 
 incremental code generation pipeline that only rebuilds what 
 has changed .

**Composes**: Resource, KindSystem, BuildCache, GenerationPlan, Emitter
**Required syncs**: resource-kind-classify, resource-cache-check, cache-plan-skip, plan-emitter-write, kind-plan-order

**Surface**:
- `build` &rarr; Resource/scan
- `emit` &rarr; Emitter/write
- `invalidate` &rarr; BuildCache/invalidate

#### Resource [R]

> Track input resources to generation pipelines : files , configs , 
 environment facts . Each resource has a content digest for change 
 detection . Centralizes what are my sources and which changed? 
 so downstream systems ( caching , planning , invalidation ) have a 
 single source of truth about inputs .

**State**:
- `resources: Set<R>`
- `locator: R Ôćĺ String`
- `kind: R Ôćĺ String`
- `digest: R Ôćĺ String`
- `lastModified: R Ôćĺ DateTime?`
- `size: R Ôćĺ Int?`

**Actions**:
- `upsert(locator: String, kind: String, digest: String, lastModified: DateTime?, size: Int?)` &rarr; created | changed | unchanged
- `get(locator: String)` &rarr; ok | notFound
- `list(kind: String?)` &rarr; ok
- `remove(locator: String)` &rarr; ok | notFound
- `diff(locator: String, oldDigest: String, newDigest: String)` &rarr; ok | unknown

#### KindSystem [K]

> Define the taxonomy of intermediate representations and 
 artifacts in generation pipelines . Track which kinds can 
 transform into which others . Enable pipeline validation , 
 execution ordering , and cascading invalidation without 
 any concept needing to know the full taxonomy .

**State**:
- `kinds: Set<K>`
- `name: K Ôćĺ String`
- `category: K Ôćĺ String`
- `edges: K Ôćĺ Set<{ target: K, relation: String, transformName: String? }>`

**Actions**:
- `define(name: String, category: String)` &rarr; ok | exists
- `connect(from: K, to: K, relation: String, transformName: String?)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `route(from: K, to: K)` &rarr; ok | unreachable
- `validate(from: K, to: K)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `dependents(kind: K)` &rarr; ok
- `producers(kind: K)` &rarr; ok
- `consumers(kind: K)` &rarr; ok
- `graph()` &rarr; ok

#### BuildCache [E]

> Track input output hashes for generation steps . 
 Enable incremental rebuilds : skip generation when 
 inputs haven t changed since the last successful run . 
 Support cascading invalidation when upstream kinds change .

**State**:
- `entries: Set<E>`
- `stepKey: E Ôćĺ String`
- `inputHash: E Ôćĺ String`
- `outputHash: E Ôćĺ String`
- `outputRef: E Ôćĺ String?`
- `lastRun: E Ôćĺ DateTime`
- `sourceLocator: E Ôćĺ String?`
- `deterministic: E Ôćĺ Bool`

**Actions**:
- `check(stepKey: String, inputHash: String, deterministic: Bool)` &rarr; unchanged | changed
- `record(stepKey: String, inputHash: String, outputHash: String, outputRef: String?, sourceLocator: String?, deterministic: Bool)` &rarr; ok
- `invalidate(stepKey: String)` &rarr; ok | notFound
- `invalidateBySource(sourceLocator: String)` &rarr; ok
- `invalidateByKind(kindName: String)` &rarr; ok
- `invalidateAll()` &rarr; ok
- `status()` &rarr; ok
- `staleSteps()` &rarr; ok

#### GenerationPlan [R]

 complete , and report . Purely passive does not dispatch

#### Emitter [F]

 same input produces same hash , skip write preserves timestamps .

### ClefAccount <sub>clef-account</sub>

> Unified authentication and identity service for the Clef ecosystem . 
 Composes credential verification , role-based authorization , policy-based 
 access control , and session management into a single deployable service 
 that all other Clef apps delegate to via proxy concepts .

**Composes**: Authentication, Authorization, AccessControl, Session
**Required syncs**: auth-session, permission-check, role-on-register, admin-role-bootstrap

**Surface**:
- `register` &rarr; Authentication/register
- `login` &rarr; Authentication/login
- `logout` &rarr; Authentication/logout
- `authenticate` &rarr; Authentication/authenticate
- `grantRole` &rarr; Authorization/grantRole
- `checkAccess` &rarr; AccessControl/check

#### Authentication [U]

> Verify user identity via pluggable authentication providers . 
 Supports multiple provider backends per user , token based 
 session authentication , and credential reset flows .

**State**:
- `accounts: Set<U>`
- `providers: Set<String>`
- `credentials: U Ôćĺ String`
- `activeProvider: U Ôćĺ String`

**Actions**:
- `register(user: U, provider: String, credentials: String)` &rarr; ok | exists
- `login(user: U, credentials: String)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `logout(user: U)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `authenticate(token: String)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `resetPassword(user: U, newCredentials: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound

#### Authorization [U]

> Manage roles , permissions , and permission checking for users . 
 Roles group permissions into reusable bundles . Users are assigned 
 roles , and permission checks resolve transitively through the 
 role permission mapping .

**State**:

- `permissions: Set<String>`

- `revokePermission(role: String, permission: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `assignRole(user: U, role: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `checkPermission(user: U, permission: String)` &rarr; ok

#### AccessControl [A]

> Evaluate three valued access decisions ( allowed forbidden neutral ) 
 with cacheable results . Forbidden overrides all allowed . Policies 
 are composable via logical OR and AND combinators , enabling 
 layered access evaluation across multiple policy sources .

**State**:
- `policies: Set<A>`
- `result: A Ôćĺ String`
- `tags: A Ôćĺ String`
- `maxAge: A Ôćĺ Int`

**Actions**:
- `check(resource: String, action: String, context: String)` &rarr; ok
- `orIf(left: String, right: String)` &rarr; ok
- `andIf(left: String, right: String)` &rarr; ok

#### Session [S]

> Manage authenticated session lifecycle including creation , 
 validation , refresh , and device tracking . Each session binds 
 a user identity to a specific device and carries an opaque 
 token with a bounded lifetime .

**State**:

- `token: S Ôćĺ String`
- `device: S Ôćĺ String`
- `expiresAt: S Ôćĺ String`

- `destroy(session: S)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `destroyAll(userId: String)` &rarr; ok
- `getContext(session: S)` &rarr; ok | notfound

### ClefBootstrap <sub>clef-cli-bootstrap</sub>

> Minimal self-updating CLI binary . Checks for newer versions of the 
 full Clef CLI at startup , downloads updates from the registry , 
 atomically swaps the binary , and delegates all other commands to 
 the full CLI .

**Composes**: SelfUpdate, Fetcher, Download
**Required syncs**: check-on-start, apply-on-update-command

**Surface**:
- `checkUpdate` &rarr; SelfUpdate/check
- `applyUpdate` &rarr; SelfUpdate/apply
- `rollbackUpdate` &rarr; SelfUpdate/rollback
- `dismissUpdate` &rarr; SelfUpdate/dismiss
- `resolveDownload` &rarr; Download/resolve

#### SelfUpdate [U]

> Binary self update lifecycle . Checks for newer versions of a running 
 binary , downloads and atomically swaps the executable , and supports 
 rollback to the previous version on failure . Manages a state machine 
 from idle through checking , downloading , swapping , to done or failed .

**State**:
- `updates: Set<U>`
- `current_version: U Ôćĺ String`
- `platform: U Ôćĺ String`
- `latest_version: U Ôćĺ String?`
- `download_url: U Ôćĺ String?`
- `content_hash: U Ôćĺ String?`
- `binary_path: U Ôćĺ String?`
- `previous_binary_path: U Ôćĺ String?`
- `status: U Ôćĺ String`
- `error_message: U Ôćĺ String?`
- `checked_at: U Ôćĺ String?`

**Actions**:
- `check(current_version: String, platform: String)` &rarr; available | current | error
- `apply(update: U, binary_path: String)` &rarr; ok | hash_mismatch | permission_denied | error
- `rollback(update: U)` &rarr; ok | no_backup | error
- `dismiss(update: U)` &rarr; ok | notfound

#### Fetcher [D]

> Download package artifacts from registries and caches . Manages individual 
 and batch downloads with integrity verification , progress tracking , 
 and cancellation support .

**State**:
- `downloads: Set<D>`
- `module_id: D Ôćĺ String`
- `version: D Ôćĺ String`
- `source_url: D Ôćĺ String`
- `expected_hash: D Ôćĺ String`
- `status: D Ôćĺ String`
- `bytes_downloaded: D Ôćĺ Int`
- `bytes_total: D Ôćĺ Int`
- `error: D Ôćĺ String?`
- `started_at: D Ôćĺ String?`
- `completed_at: D Ôćĺ String?`

**Actions**:
- `fetch(module_id: String, version: String, source_url: String, expected_hash: String)` &rarr; ok | cached | integrity_failure | network_error
- `fetchBatch(items: List<{ module_id: String, version: String, source_url: String, expected_hash: String }>)` &rarr; ok | partial
- `cancel(download: D)` &rarr; ok

#### Download [D]

> Per platform binary artifact distribution . Tracks downloadable 
 artifacts by platform and version , maintains download counts , 
 and supports yanking artifacts from distribution while preserving 
 existing installations .

**State**:
- `downloads: Set<D>`
- `artifact_id: D Ôćĺ String`
- `platform: D Ôćĺ String`
- `version: D Ôćĺ String`
- `content_hash: D Ôćĺ String`
- `artifact_url: D Ôćĺ String`
- `size_bytes: D Ôćĺ Int`
- `download_count: D Ôćĺ Int`
- `yanked: D Ôćĺ Bool`
- `registered_at: D Ôćĺ String`

**Actions**:
- `register(artifact_id: String, platform: String, version: String, content_hash: String, artifact_url: String, size_bytes: Int)` &rarr; ok | exists | invalid
- `resolve(artifact_id: String, platform: String, version_range: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound | yanked
- `yank(download: D)` &rarr; ok | notfound | already_yanked
- `stats(artifact_id: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound

### ConversationalRAG <sub>llm-conversation</sub>

> Combine retrieval-augmented generation with multi-turn conversation 
 management and prompt engineering to enable context-aware dialogue 
 grounded in retrieved documents .

**Composes**: RAGPipeline _(derived)_, Conversation, PromptPipeline _(derived)_
**Required syncs**: conversation-retrieval, retrieval-prompt-inject, conversation-context-window

**Surface**:
- `ask` &rarr; RAGPipeline/retrieve
- `respond` &rarr; Conversation/append
- `assembleWithContext` &rarr; PromptPipeline/assemble

#### Conversation [C]

> Persistent , branching sequence of messages representing a dialogue 
 thread . Manages appending , forking for exploration ( Loom multiversal 
 branching ) , truncating to fit context windows , and summarizing old 
 context . The session manager for LLM interactions . Tree DAG structure 
 eliminates context pollution by scoping each branch to its own lineage .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `conversations: Set<C>`
- `messages: C Ôćĺ List<{ id: String, role: String, content: String, parts: List<{ type: String, data: String }>?, tool_calls: List<{ id: String, function_name: String, arguments: String }>?, metadata: { model: String, tokens: Int, cost: Float, finish_reason: String }?, timestamp: DateTime }>`
- `branches: C Ôćĺ List<{ branch_id: String, parent_message_id: String, message_ids: List<String> }>`
- `active_branch: C Ôćĺ String?`
- `context_strategy: C Ôćĺ String`
- `summary: C Ôćĺ String?`
- `node_metadata: C Ôćĺ List<{ message_id: String, model_params: String?, logprobs: String? }>`
- `created_at: C Ôćĺ DateTime`
- `updated_at: C Ôćĺ DateTime`
- `participant_ids: C Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `tags: C Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `token_count: C Ôćĺ Int`

**Actions**:
- `create(context_strategy: String)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `append(conversation: C, role: String, content: String, parts: List<{ type: String, data: String }>?, tool_calls: List<{ id: String, function_name: String, arguments: String }>?, metadata: { model: String, tokens: Int, cost: Float, finish_reason: String }?)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `fork(conversation: C, from_message_id: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `switchBranch(conversation: C, branch_id: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `merge(conversation: C, branch_ids: List<String>, strategy: String)` &rarr; ok | conflict
- `prune(conversation: C, branch_id: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `getContextWindow(conversation: C, max_tokens: Int)` &rarr; ok | empty
- `summarize(conversation: C, message_ids: List<String>)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `getLineage(conversation: C, message_id: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `serialize(conversation: C, format: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound

#### RAGPipeline <sub>llm-rag</sub>

> Compose document chunking , vector indexing , and retrieval into 
 a complete retrieval-augmented generation pipeline .

**Composes**: DocumentChunk, VectorIndex, Retriever
**Required syncs**: chunk-to-embed, embed-to-index, index-to-retriever

**Surface**:
- `indexDocument` &rarr; DocumentChunk/split
- `search` &rarr; VectorIndex/search
- `retrieve` &rarr; Retriever/retrieve

##### DocumentChunk [D]

> Segment of a larger document with metadata , embeddings , and relationship 
 links . Bridge between raw content and vector search . Encapsulates 
 chunking strategies central to RAG quality : recursive , semantic , 
 sentence , fixed size , structural , agentic .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `chunks: Set<D>`
- `text: D Ôćĺ String`
- `metadata: D Ôćĺ { source_document_id: String, position: Int, page_number: Int?, section_title: String? }`
- `embedding: D Ôćĺ List<Float>?`
- `relationships: D Ôćĺ { parent_document_id: String, prev_chunk_id: String?, next_chunk_id: String?, child_chunk_ids: List<String> }`
- `chunk_strategy: D Ôćĺ String`
- `token_count: D Ôćĺ Int`

**Actions**:
- `split(document_id: String, content: String, strategy: String, config: { chunk_size: Int, chunk_overlap: Int })` &rarr; ok | error
- `enrich(chunk: D, extractors: List<String>)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `getContext(chunk: D, window_size: Int)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `getParent(chunk: D)` &rarr; ok | notfound

##### VectorIndex [X]

> Stores embedding vectors with metadata and provides similarity search . 
 The database of the RAG stack . Abstracts over backends from in process 
 FAISS to managed Pinecone to pgvector . Supports hybrid search combining 
 vector similarity with keyword search via reciprocal rank fusion . 
 Manages its own embedding configuration ( model , dimensions ) since 
 Embedding was absorbed here .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `indexes: Set<X>`
- `dimensions: X Ôćĺ Int`
- `distance_metric: X Ôćĺ String`
- `index_type: X Ôćĺ String`
- `backend: X Ôćĺ String`
- `embedding_model: X Ôćĺ String`
- `collections: X Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `document_count: X Ôćĺ Int`
- `index_config: X Ôćĺ String?`

**Actions**:
- `create(dimensions: Int, distance_metric: String, index_type: String, backend: String, embedding_model: String)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `embed(index: X, text: String)` &rarr; ok | error
- `embedBatch(index: X, texts: List<String>)` &rarr; ok | partial
- `add(index: X, id: String, vector: List<Float>, metadata: String?)` &rarr; ok | dimension_mismatch
- `addBatch(index: X, items: List<{ id: String, vector: List<Float>, metadata: String? }>)` &rarr; ok | partial
- `search(index: X, query_vector: List<Float>, k: Int, filters: String?)` &rarr; ok | empty
- `hybridSearch(index: X, query_vector: List<Float>, keyword_query: String, vector_weight: Float, k: Int)` &rarr; ok | empty

##### Retriever [R]

> RAG orchestration layer . Takes natural language query , finds relevant 
 content , prepares for LLM consumption . Multi stage pipeline : 
 first stage retrieval ( fast , high recall ) then re ranking ( accurate ) 
 then compression . Supports multi query expansion , self query metadata 
 filtering , contextual compression , and hierarchical retrieval .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `retrievers: Set<R>`
- `retriever_type: R Ôćĺ String`
- `source_ids: R Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `top_k: R Ôćĺ Int`
- `reranker_config: R Ôćĺ { model: String, top_n: Int }?`
- `filters: R Ôćĺ String?`
- `score_threshold: R Ôćĺ Float?`

**Actions**:
- `create(retriever_type: String, source_ids: List<String>, top_k: Int, score_threshold: Float?)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `retrieve(retriever: R, query: String)` &rarr; ok | empty
- `multiQueryRetrieve(retriever: R, query: String)` &rarr; ok | empty
- `selfQueryRetrieve(retriever: R, query: String)` &rarr; ok | empty

#### PromptPipeline <sub>llm-prompt</sub>

> Compose prompt assembly , few-shot example selection , optimization , 
 and LLM provider routing into a complete prompt engineering pipeline .

**Composes**: PromptAssembly, FewShotExample, PromptOptimizer, LLMProvider
**Required syncs**: assembly-examples, assembly-optimizer, assembly-provider

**Surface**:
- `assemble` &rarr; PromptAssembly/assemble
- `selectExamples` &rarr; FewShotExample/select
- `optimize` &rarr; PromptOptimizer/optimize
- `generate` &rarr; LLMProvider/generate

##### PromptAssembly [P]

> Composes a complete LLM prompt from independent sections : system 
 instructions , persona directives , few shot examples , retrieved context , 
 user input , and output format directives . The layout manager handles 
 structural semantics , section ordering , token allocation per section , 
 priority based truncation under budget pressure , and the rendering 
 pipeline . Absorbs token budget management : each section has a 
 max_tokens allocation and priority ; when total exceeds the context 
 window , lowest priority sections are truncated first .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `assemblies: Set<P>`
- `sections: P Ôćĺ List<{ name: String, role: String, template_ref: String?, priority: Int, max_tokens: Int, required: Bool, content: String? }>`
- `assembly_strategy: P Ôćĺ String`
- `format: P Ôćĺ String`
- `variables: P Ôćĺ List<{ name: String, value: String }>`
- `output_directive: P Ôćĺ String?`
- `tokenizer_id: P Ôćĺ String`
- `context_window: P Ôćĺ Int`

**Actions**:
- `create(strategy: String, format: String, tokenizer_id: String, context_window: Int)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `addSection(assembly: P, name: String, role: String, priority: Int, max_tokens: Int, required: Bool, content: String?, template_ref: String?)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `setVariable(assembly: P, name: String, value: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `assemble(assembly: P)` &rarr; ok | over_budget
- `toMessages(assembly: P)` &rarr; ok | over_budget
- `estimateTokens(assembly: P)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `removeSection(assembly: P, name: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound

##### FewShotExample [F]

> Manages pools of input output examples and selects the most effective 
 subset for each prompt at runtime . Supports semantic similarity , maximal 
 marginal relevance , bootstrapped , and length based selection . 2 -5 
 examples is optimal ; beyond 5 returns diminish . Last example weighted 
 most heavily due to recency bias .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `pools: Set<F>`
- `examples: F Ôćĺ List<{ id: String, input: String, output: String, metadata: String?, embedding: List<Float>? }>`
- `selection_strategy: F Ôćĺ String`
- `k: F Ôćĺ Int`
- `diversity_weight: F Ôćĺ Float`
- `quality_scores: F Ôćĺ List<{ id: String, score: Float }>`

**Actions**:
- `createPool(strategy: String, k: Int, diversity_weight: Float)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `add(pool: F, input: String, output: String, metadata: String?)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `select(pool: F, input: String, k: Int?)` &rarr; ok | empty
- `optimize(pool: F, metric: String, training_set: List<{ input: String, expected: String }>)` &rarr; ok | error
- `embed(pool: F, model_id: String)` &rarr; ok | error
- `remove(pool: F, example_id: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound

##### PromptOptimizer [O]

> Automatically improves prompts using LLM driven optimization , treating 
 prompt text as a learnable parameter . DSPy paradigm : programming , not 
 prompting . Supports BootstrapFewShot , MIPROv2 , COPRO , OPRO , and 
 evolutionary strategies .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage, network

**State**:

- `metric: O Ôćĺ String`
- `training_set: O Ôćĺ List<{ input: String, expected: String }>`

- `best_candidate: O Ôćĺ { prompt: String, score: Float }?`
- `budget: O Ôćĺ { max_llm_calls: Int, used_calls: Int }`

**Actions**:

- `optimize(optimizer: O)` &rarr; ok | budget_exceeded | error

##### LLMProvider [P]

> Atomic gateway to any large language model . Wraps provider specific 
 APIs behind a uniform interface for completion , streaming , embedding , 
 and token counting . Stateless per call : holds configuration and 
 credentials but no conversation history .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage, network

**State**:
- `providers: Set<P>`
- `provider_id: P Ôćĺ String`
- `model_id: P Ôćĺ String`
- `api_credentials: P Ôćĺ Bytes`
- `default_config: P Ôćĺ { temperature: Float, top_p: Float, max_tokens: Int, stop_sequences: List<String> }`
- `capabilities: P Ôćĺ Set<String>`
- `pricing: P Ôćĺ { input_cost_per_token: Float, output_cost_per_token: Float, cached_cost_per_token: Float? }`
- `rate_limits: P Ôćĺ { requests_per_minute: Int, tokens_per_minute: Int }`
- `status: P Ôćĺ String`

**Actions**:
- `register(provider_id: String, model_id: String, credentials: Bytes, config: { temperature: Float, top_p: Float, max_tokens: Int, stop_sequences: List<String> }, capabilities: Set<String>)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `generate(provider: P, messages: List<{ role: String, content: String }>, config: { temperature: Float, top_p: Float, max_tokens: Int }?)` &rarr; ok | rate_limited | context_overflow | auth_failure | content_filtered | unavailable
- `stream(provider: P, messages: List<{ role: String, content: String }>, config: { temperature: Float, top_p: Float, max_tokens: Int }?)` &rarr; ok | rate_limited | unavailable
- `embed(provider: P, texts: List<String>)` &rarr; ok | error
- `countTokens(provider: P, content: String)` &rarr; ok | error
- `healthCheck(provider: P)` &rarr; ok | degraded | unavailable
- `updateConfig(provider: P, config: { temperature: Float, top_p: Float, max_tokens: Int, stop_sequences: List<String> })` &rarr; ok | notfound

### DeployPipeline <sub>framework</sub>

> Compose deployment planning , progressive rollout , schema 
 migration , health checking , and environment management into

 and automated rollback .

**Composes**: DeployPlan, Rollout, Migration, Health, Env

- `advance` &rarr; Rollout/advance

- `abort` &rarr; Rollout/abort

#### DeployPlan [D]

> Compute , validate , and execute deployment plans for suites . 
 Constructs a dependency graph from concept specs , syncs , 
 and the deploy manifest , then executes operations in 
 topological order with parallelism on independent branches .

**State**:

- `failedNodes: D Ôćĺ List<String>`

**Actions**:

- `status(plan: D)` &rarr; ok | notfound

#### Rollout [R]

> Manage progressive delivery of concept deployments . 
 Controls traffic splitting between old and new versions , 
 monitors health between steps , and triggers rollback on 
 failure . Strategies : canary , blue green , rolling .

**State**:

- `autoRollback: R Ôćĺ Bool`
- `currentStep: R Ôćĺ Int`
- `currentWeight: R Ôćĺ Int`
- `startedAt: R Ôćĺ DateTime`
- `status: R Ôćĺ String`
- `oldVersion: R Ôćĺ String`
- `newVersion: R Ôćĺ String`
- `plan: R Ôćĺ String`

**Actions**:
- `begin(plan: String, strategy: String, steps: List<String>)` &rarr; ok | invalidStrategy
- `advance(rollout: R)` &rarr; ok | complete | paused
- `pause(rollout: R, reason: String)` &rarr; ok
- `resume(rollout: R)` &rarr; ok
- `abort(rollout: R)` &rarr; ok | alreadyComplete
- `status(rollout: R)` &rarr; ok

#### Migration [M]

> Orchestrate storage schema migrations for concepts whose 
 version has changed . Uses the expand contract pattern : 
 expand adds new schema alongside old , migrate copies data 
 with dual write , contract removes old schema . Each phase 
 is a gate blocking deployment until it passes .

**State**:
- `migrations: Set<M>`
- `concept: M Ôćĺ String`
- `fromVersion: M Ôćĺ Int`
- `toVersion: M Ôćĺ Int`
- `phase: M Ôćĺ String`
- `recordsMigrated: M Ôćĺ Int`
- `recordsTotal: M Ôćĺ Int`
- `startedAt: M Ôćĺ DateTime`
- `errors: M Ôćĺ List<String>`

**Actions**:
- `plan(concept: String, fromVersion: Int, toVersion: Int)` &rarr; ok | noMigrationNeeded | incompatible
- `expand(migration: M)` &rarr; ok | failed
- `migrate(migration: M)` &rarr; ok | partial
- `contract(migration: M)` &rarr; ok | rollback
- `status(migration: M)` &rarr; ok

#### Health [H]

> Verify deployment health at concept , sync , and suite levels . 
 Used as a gate in progressive delivery so rollout advances 
 only when health checks pass . Also provides ongoing 
 monitoring after deployment completes .

**State**:

- `checkSync(sync: String, concepts: List<String>)` &rarr; ok | partialFailure | timeout
- `checkKit(suite: String, environment: String)` &rarr; ok | degraded | failed
- `checkInvariant(concept: String, invariant: String)` &rarr; ok | violated

#### Env [E]

 Base environment defines defaults ; overlays for dev , staging ,

**Required syncs**: asset-file-link, asset-tag-classify, asset-collection-membership, file-thumbnail

**Surface**:
- `upload` &rarr; MediaAsset/createMedia
- `tag` &rarr; Tag/addTag
- `addToCollection` &rarr; Collection/addMember

### MigrationPlan <sub>deployment</sub>

> Coordinate schema migrations with deployment plans to ensure

### NewApp <sub>new-app</sub>

> End-to-end orchestration of new project creation . Apps are 
 built from data and content primitives drawn from the 
 Repertoire s Foundation , Content , Data-Integration , and 
 Data-Organization suites , ensuring every project starts with 
 structured storage , content modeling , and data pipeline 
 capabilities . Composes template browsing , target profiling , 
 module selection , project scaffolding , and the full package 
 management pipeline ( resolve , fetch , install ) into a single 
 coordinated workflow that takes a user from I want a social
    app to a runnable project on disk .

**Composes**: AppTemplate, TargetProfile, ModuleSelection, ProjectInit, Manifest, Resolver, Lockfile, Fetcher, ContentStore, Installer, ContentNode, ContentStorage, Outline, Property, TypeSystem, PageAsRecord, ContentParser, Intent, Comment, Template, Canvas, Version, DailyNote, SyncedContent, DataSource, Connector, Capture, FieldMapping, Transform, Enricher, SyncPair, DataQuality, Provenance, ProgressiveSchema, Collection, Graph
**Required syncs**: template-to-selection, profile-to-selection, selection-to-init, init-scaffold-chain, init-to-package-chain, install-to-generate, generate-to-complete

**Surface**:
- `createFromTemplate` &rarr; AppTemplate/customize
- `createCustom` &rarr; ModuleSelection/begin
- `browseTemplates` &rarr; AppTemplate/list
- `configureTargets` &rarr; TargetProfile/validate
- `previewProject` &rarr; ModuleSelection/preview

#### AppTemplate [T]

> Curated starting configurations that bundle related concepts , 
 syncs , derived concepts , and feature defaults into named 
 templates . Templates compose data and content primitives from 
 the Repertoire s Foundation , Content , Data Integration , and 
 Data Organization suites , giving each new project structured 
 storage , content modeling , and data pipeline capabilities out 
 of the box . Enables rapid project bootstrapping by category 
 while allowing customization of the included module set .

**State**:
- `templates: Set<T>`
- `name: T Ôćĺ String`
- `description: T Ôćĺ String`
- `category: T Ôćĺ {social | cms | ecommerce | api | tool}`
- `included_modules: T Ôćĺ List<{ module_id: String, kind: String, required: Bool, rationale: String }>`
- `included_syncs: T Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `suggested_derived: T Ôćĺ List<{ name: String, composes: List<String> }>`
- `default_features: T Ôćĺ List<{ module_id: String, features: List<String> }>`
- `compatible_languages: T Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `compatible_platforms: T Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `minimum_concepts: T Ôćĺ Int`

**Actions**:
- `list(category: String?)` &rarr; ok
- `detail(name: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `customize(template: T, add: List<String>, remove: List<String>, features: List<String>)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `register(name: String, description: String, category: String, modules: List<String>, syncs: List<String>)` &rarr; ok | duplicate

- `frontend_frameworks: P Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `api_interfaces: P Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `sdk_languages: P Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `deploy_targets: P Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `storage_adapters: P Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `transport_adapters: P Ôćĺ List<String>`

**Actions**:
- `create(name: String)` &rarr; ok
- `setBackendLanguages(profile: P, languages: List<String>)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `setFrontendFrameworks(profile: P, frameworks: List<String>)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `setApiInterfaces(profile: P, interfaces: List<String>)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `setSdkLanguages(profile: P, languages: List<String>)` &rarr; ok

- `setStorageAdapters(profile: P, adapters: List<String>)` &rarr; ok

- `listOptions()` &rarr; ok

#### ModuleSelection [S]

> Compute the complete set of modules needed for a new project 
 by combining template defaults , target profile requirements , 
 and manual selections . Tracks concepts , syncs , handlers , 
 widgets , themes , bind targets , SDK providers , deploy providers , 
 and derived concepts , then flattens everything into a final 
 module list for installation .

**State**:
- `selections: Set<S>`
- `template_name: S Ôćĺ String?`
- `profile_name: S Ôćĺ String?`
- `selected_concepts: S Ôćĺ List<{ module_id: String, source: String }>`
- `selected_syncs: S Ôćĺ List<{ module_id: String, source: String }>`
- `selected_handlers: S Ôćĺ List<{ concept_module: String, handler_module: String, language: String }>`
- `selected_widgets: S Ôćĺ List<{ module_id: String, source: String }>`
- `selected_themes: S Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `selected_bind_targets: S Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `selected_sdk_providers: S Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `selected_deploy_providers: S Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `derived_concepts: S Ôćĺ List<{ name: String, composes: List<String> }>`
- `all_modules: S Ôćĺ List<{ module_id: String, kind: String, version_range: String, features: List<String>, source: String }>`

**Actions**:
- `begin(template_name: String?, profile_name: String?)` &rarr; ok | template_notfound | profile_notfound
- `addConcept(selection: S, module_id: String, features: List<String>)` &rarr; ok | already_selected
- `removeConcept(selection: S, module_id: String)` &rarr; ok | required | has_dependents
- `chooseHandler(selection: S, concept_module: String, handler_module: String)` &rarr; ok | incompatible | language_mismatch
- `addWidget(selection: S, module_id: String)` &rarr; ok
- `selectTheme(selection: S, theme_module: String)` &rarr; ok
- `addDerived(selection: S, name: String, composes: List<String>)` &rarr; ok | missing_concepts
- `finalize(selection: S)` &rarr; ok | incomplete
- `preview(selection: S)` &rarr; ok

#### ProjectInit [J]

 dependency installation , and code generation , tracking status 
 through each stage .

- `profile: J Ôćĺ { backend_languages: List<String>, frontend_frameworks: List<String>, api_interfaces: List<String>, deploy_targets: List<String> }`
- `derived_concepts: J Ôćĺ List<{ name: String, composes: List<String> }>`
- `status: J Ôćĺ {pending | scaffolding | resolving | installing | generating | complete | failed}`
- `error: J Ôćĺ String?`
- `created_files: J Ôćĺ List<String>`

**Actions**:

- `triggerGenerate(init: J)` &rarr; ok | error
- `complete(init: J)` &rarr; ok

#### Manifest [P]

> Declarative project configuration file . Describes a project s identity , 
 dependency requirements with version ranges and feature selections , 
 registry sources , dependency overrides , patches , and target platform 
 constraints . Serves as the human authored input to the Resolver .

**State**:
- `projects: Set<P>`
- `name: P Ôćĺ String`
- `version: P Ôćĺ String`
- `dependencies: P Ôćĺ List<{ module_id: String, version_range: String, edge_type: String, environment: String, features: List<String>, optional: Bool }>`
- `overrides: P Ôćĺ List<{ module_id: String, replacement_id: String?, replacement_source: String?, version_pin: String? }>`
- `patches: P Ôćĺ List<{ target_module: String, patch_path: String }>`
- `disabled: P Ôćĺ Set<String>`
- `resolution_policy: P Ôćĺ { unification_strategy: String, feature_unification: String, prefer_locked: Bool, allowed_updates: String }`
- `registries: P Ôćĺ List<{ name: String, url: String, scope: String? }>`
- `target_languages: P Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `target_platforms: P Ôćĺ List<String>`

**Actions**:
- `add(project: P, module_id: String, version_range: String, edge_type: String, environment: String, features: List<String>, optional: Bool)` &rarr; ok | exists | invalid
- `remove(project: P, module_id: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `override(project: P, module_id: String, replacement_id: String?, replacement_source: String?, version_pin: String?)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `disable(project: P, module_id: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `enable(project: P, module_id: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `merge(base: P, overlay: P)` &rarr; ok | conflict
- `validate(project: P)` &rarr; ok | invalid

#### Resolver [R]

> PubGrub based conflict driven dependency solver . Accepts a set of input 
 constraints and a resolution policy , then produces a fully resolved module 
 graph with exact versions , content hashes , and enabled features . Provides 
 human readable conflict explanations when resolution is unsolvable .

**State**:
- `resolutions: Set<R>`
- `input_constraints: R Ôćĺ List<{ module_id: String, version_range: String, edge_type: String, environment: String, features: List<String> }>`
- `resolved_modules: R Ôćĺ List<{ module_id: String, resolved_version: String, content_hash: String, features_enabled: List<String> }>`
- `resolution_policy: R Ôćĺ { unification_strategy: String, feature_unification: String, prefer_locked: Bool, allowed_updates: String }`
- `conflict_explanation: R Ôćĺ String?`
- `status: R Ôćĺ String`

**Actions**:
- `resolve(constraints: List<{ module_id: String, version_range: String, edge_type: String, environment: String, features: List<String> }>, policy: { unification_strategy: String, feature_unification: String, prefer_locked: Bool, allowed_updates: String }, locked_versions: List<{ module_id: String, version: String, content_hash: String }>?)` &rarr; ok | unsolvable | error
- `update(resolution: R, targets: List<String>, policy: { unification_strategy: String, feature_unification: String, prefer_locked: Bool, allowed_updates: String })` &rarr; ok | unsolvable
- `explain(resolution: R, module_id: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound

#### Lockfile [L]

> Serialized resolved dependency graph . Captures the exact module versions , 
 content hashes , artifact URLs , and enabled features from a successful 
 resolution , ensuring deterministic and reproducible installations across 
 environments . Supports integrity verification and diffing between versions .

**State**:
- `lockfiles: Set<L>`
- `project_hash: L Ôćĺ String`
- `entries: L Ôćĺ List<{ module_id: String, version: String, content_hash: String, artifact_url: String, integrity: String, features_enabled: List<String>, dependencies: List<String> }>`
- `metadata: L Ôćĺ { resolver_version: String, resolved_at: String, registry_snapshot: String }`

**Actions**:
- `write(project_hash: String, entries: List<{ module_id: String, version: String, content_hash: String, artifact_url: String, integrity: String, features_enabled: List<String>, dependencies: List<String> }>, metadata: { resolver_version: String, resolved_at: String, registry_snapshot: String })` &rarr; ok | error
- `read(lockfile: L)` &rarr; ok | notfound | corrupt
- `verify(lockfile: L)` &rarr; ok | stale | tampered
- `diff(old_lockfile: L, new_lockfile: L)` &rarr; ok | error

#### ContentStore [B]

> Content addressed blob storage for package artifacts . Deduplicates 
 identical content via cryptographic hashing , tracks reference counts , 
 and supports garbage collection of unreferenced blobs .

**State**:
- `blobs: Set<B>`
- `hash: B Ôćĺ String`
- `size: B Ôćĺ Int`
- `media_type: B Ôćĺ String`
- `stored_at: B Ôćĺ String`
- `storage_path: B Ôćĺ String`
- `reference_count: B Ôćĺ Int`

**Actions**:
- `store(data: Bytes, media_type: String)` &rarr; ok | error
- `retrieve(hash: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `verify(hash: String)` &rarr; ok | corrupted
- `gc(lockfile_hashes: List<String>)` &rarr; ok
- `stats()` &rarr; ok

#### Installer [I]

> Staged transactional installation of resolved packages . Each installation 
 is an immutable generation that can be atomically activated or rolled back . 
 Supports generational cleanup to reclaim disk space .

**State**:

- `generation: I Ôćĺ Int`
- `lockfile_hash: I Ôćĺ String`
- `staged_modules: I Ôćĺ List<{ module_id: String, version: String, content_hash: String, target_path: String, kind: String }>`
- `active: I Ôćĺ Bool`
- `previous_generation: I Ôćĺ I?`
- `installed_at: I Ôćĺ String?`

**Actions**:
- `stage(lockfile_entries: List<{ module_id: String, version: String, content_hash: String, target_path: String, kind: String }>, project_root: String)` &rarr; ok | error
- `activate(installation: I)` &rarr; ok | error
- `rollback(installation: I)` &rarr; ok | no_previous
- `clean(keep_generations: Int)` &rarr; ok

- `compareWindows(symbol: String, windowA: String, windowB: String)` &rarr; ok | insufficientData
- `get(profile: P)` &rarr; ok | notfound

#### ErrorCorrelation [E]

> Links runtime errors to their static context which concept , 
 action , variant , sync , widget , file , and line produced the 
 error , and what was the state of the flow at failure time . 
 The root_cause action walks backward through the flow to find 
 the earliest deviation from the expected FlowGraph path .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `errors: Set<E>`
- `flowId: E Ôćĺ String`
- `timestamp: E Ôćĺ String`
- `errorKind: E Ôćĺ String`
- `errorMessage: E Ôćĺ String`
- `stackTrace: E Ôćĺ String`
- `conceptEntity: E Ôćĺ String`
- `actionEntity: E Ôćĺ String`
- `variantEntity: E Ôćĺ String`
- `syncEntity: E Ôćĺ String`
- `widgetEntity: E Ôćĺ String`
- `sourceLocation: E Ôćĺ String`
- `flowContext: E Ôćĺ String`

**Actions**:
- `record(flowId: String, errorKind: String, message: String, rawEvent: String)` &rarr; ok
- `findByEntity(symbol: String, since: String)` &rarr; ok
- `findByKind(errorKind: String, since: String)` &rarr; ok

- `get(error: E)` &rarr; ok | notfound

### SafeAgent <sub>llm-agent</sub>

> Wrap an agent execution loop with tool safety guardrails and 
 observability tracing to ensure controlled , auditable agent behavior .

**Composes**: AgentLoop, ToolBinding, Guardrail, LLMTrace
**Required syncs**: agent-tool-binding, agent-guardrail-check, agent-trace-span

**Surface**:
- `run` &rarr; AgentLoop/run
- `invoke` &rarr; ToolBinding/invoke
- `checkSafety` &rarr; Guardrail/check

#### AgentLoop [L] `@gate`

> Coordination concept for agent reasoning cycles . Defines the interface 
 contract for agent execution : create , run , step , observe , interrupt , 
 resume . Strategy providers ( React , PlanAndExecute , etc . ) register 
 themselves with PluginRegistry independently . AgentLoop has zero 
 awareness of which providers exist routing syncs resolve a strategy 
 string to the correct provider at call time via PluginRegistry .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `agents: Set<L>`
- `available_tools: L Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `max_iterations: L Ôćĺ Int`
- `current_step: L Ôćĺ Int`
- `status: L Ôćĺ String`
- `goal: L Ôćĺ String?`

**Actions**:
- `create(available_tools: List<String>, max_iterations: Int)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `run(agent: L, goal: String, context: String, strategy: String)` &rarr; ok | max_iterations | error | waiting_for_human
- `step(agent: L)` &rarr; thought | action_request | final_answer | error
- `observe(agent: L, observation: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `interrupt(agent: L)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `resume(agent: L, human_input: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound

#### ToolBinding [T]

> Callable tools functions that LLMs can invoke . Unifies OpenAI function 
 calling , Anthropic tool use , and MCP tool primitive . Full lifecycle : 
 schema definition , provider format translation , argument validation , 
 execution , result formatting , error handling . Supports dynamic tool 
 selection for large tool sets and safety annotations per MCP spec .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `tools: Set<T>`
- `name: T Ôćĺ String`
- `description: T Ôćĺ String`
- `input_schema: T Ôćĺ String`
- `output_schema: T Ôćĺ String?`
- `handler: T Ôćĺ String`
- `annotations: T Ôćĺ { audience: String, destructive: Bool, idempotent: Bool, open_world: Bool }`
- `timeout_ms: T Ôćĺ Int`
- `retry_policy: T Ôćĺ { max_retries: Int, backoff_ms: Int }`
- `requires_approval: T Ôćĺ Bool`

**Actions**:
- `define(name: String, description: String, input_schema: String, output_schema: String?, handler: String, annotations: { audience: String, destructive: Bool, idempotent: Bool, open_world: Bool }, timeout_ms: Int, requires_approval: Bool)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `invoke(tool: T, arguments: String)` &rarr; ok | validation_error | timeout | execution_error | approval_required
- `toProviderFormat(tool: T, provider: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `discover(filter: { audience: String?, destructive: Bool? }?)` &rarr; ok
- `search(query: String, k: Int)` &rarr; ok | empty

#### Guardrail [G]

> Safety enforcement layer that validates LLM inputs and outputs against 
 configurable rules . Supports content filtering ( toxicity , PII , prompt 
 injection ) , topic restrictions , format validation , and custom predicate 
 checks . Runs both pre generation ( input guardrails ) and post generation 
 ( output guardrails ) . Actions are idempotent safety checks that never 
 modify the content they only pass , flag , or block .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `guardrails: Set<G>`
- `name: G Ôćĺ String`
- `guardrail_type: G Ôćĺ String`
- `config: G Ôćĺ { threshold: Float, action_on_violation: String, categories: List<String> }`
- `rules: G Ôćĺ List<{ id: String, pattern: String, severity: String }>`
- `violation_log: G Ôćĺ List<{ timestamp: DateTime, input_hash: String, rule_id: String, severity: String, action_taken: String }>`

**Actions**:
- `create(name: String, guardrail_type: String, config: { threshold: Float, action_on_violation: String, categories: List<String> })` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `addRule(guardrail: G, pattern: String, severity: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `checkInput(guardrail: G, message: String)` &rarr; pass | violation
- `checkOutput(guardrail: G, response: String)` &rarr; pass | violation
- `check(guardrail: G, content: String, direction: String)` &rarr; pass | blocked | flagged
- `getViolations(guardrail: G, filters: { after: DateTime?, severity: String? }?)` &rarr; ok | empty
- `removeRule(guardrail: G, rule_id: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound

#### LLMTrace [Z]

> Observability for LLM execution pipelines . Captures hierarchical 
 trace spans covering every LLM call , tool invocation , retrieval 
 operation , and agent step . Tracks latency , token usage , cost , 
 and quality metrics . Enables debugging , cost analysis , and 
 performance optimization . Compatible with OpenTelemetry export .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `traces: Set<Z>`
- `name: Z Ôćĺ String`
- `spans: Z Ôćĺ List<{ id: String, parent_id: String?, operation: String, start_time: DateTime, end_time: DateTime?, status: String, metadata: String? }>`
- `metrics: Z Ôćĺ List<{ span_id: String, key: String, value: Float }>`
- `tags: Z Ôćĺ List<{ key: String, value: String }>`
- `total_cost: Z Ôćĺ Float`
- `total_tokens: Z Ôćĺ Int`

**Actions**:
- `startTrace(name: String, tags: List<{ key: String, value: String }>)` &rarr; ok | error
- `startSpan(trace: Z, operation: String, parent_span_id: String?)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `endSpan(trace: Z, span_id: String, status: String, metrics: { tokens: Int, cost: Float, latency_ms: Int }?)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `addMetric(trace: Z, span_id: String, key: String, value: Float)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `getCost(trace: Z)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `getTrace(trace: Z)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `export(trace: Z, format: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound

#### Sdk [S]

 tracking . Generator talks to Sdk , never to language

 GraphQL , gRPC , CLI , MCP ) . Owns the target registry , output

**Actions**:

- `diff(output: T)` &rarr; ok | noPrevious

#### Annotation [N]

> Attach arbitrary metadata to concepts and actions for 
 interface generation . The concept owns identity ( which 
 concept , which scope ) and opaque content passthrough . 
 Each target reads the keys it understands and ignores 
 the rest . New enrichment kinds require only a new YAML 
 key and a renderer in the target provider zero concept 
 changes . See Architecture doc Section 1.8 .

### SemanticWidgetSelection <sub>semantic</sub>

> Select the best widget for a UI element by matching interactor 
 semantics against declared affordances and resolving through 
 weighted scoring .

**Composes**: InteractorEntity, Affordance, WidgetResolver
**Required syncs**: interactor-affordance-match, affordance-resolver-score, resolver-widget-bind

**Surface**:
- `selectWidget` &rarr; WidgetResolver/resolve
- `declareAffordance` &rarr; Affordance/declare

#### InteractorEntity [I]

> Queryable representation of a registered interactor type 
 the abstract interaction taxonomy as a traversable node . 
 Enables queries like what fields classify as this interactor? 
 and what widgets match this interactor in a given context?

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `interactors: Set<I>`
- `name: I Ôćĺ String`
- `symbol: I Ôćĺ String`
- `category: I Ôćĺ String`
- `properties: I Ôćĺ String`
- `classificationRules: I Ôćĺ String`

- `findByCategory(category: String)` &rarr; ok
- `matchingWidgets(interactor: I, context: String)` &rarr; ok
- `classifiedFields(interactor: I)` &rarr; ok
- `coverageReport()` &rarr; ok
- `get(interactor: I)` &rarr; ok | notfound

#### Affordance [F]

> Declare what semantic interaction situations a widget 
 can serve . Each affordance binds a widget name to an 
 interactor type with conditional constraints . A widget 
 may have multiple affordances at different specificity 
 levels . The most specific matching affordance wins . 
 Affordances are declared in . widget file affordance 
 sections and registered by WidgetParser .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `affordances: Set<F>`
- `widget: F Ôćĺ String`
- `interactor: F Ôćĺ String`
- `specificity: F Ôćĺ Int`
- `minOptions: F Ôćĺ Int?`
- `maxOptions: F Ôćĺ Int?`
- `platform: F Ôćĺ String?`
- `viewport: F Ôćĺ String?`
- `density: F Ôćĺ String?`
- `mutable: F Ôćĺ Bool?`

**Actions**:
- `declare(affordance: F, widget: String, interactor: String, specificity: Int, conditions: String?)` &rarr; ok | duplicate
- `match(affordance: F, interactor: String, context: String)` &rarr; ok | none
- `explain(affordance: F)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `remove(affordance: F)` &rarr; ok | notfound

#### WidgetResolver [R]

> Context aware selection of the best widget for a given 
 abstract element . Gathers semantic properties from the 
 element s interactor type , combines with runtime context , 
 queries affordance declarations , and returns a ranked 
 selection . Replaces flat type mapping tables with a 
 parameterized , extensible decision engine .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `overrides: R Ôćĺ String?`
- `defaultContext: R Ôćĺ String`
- `scoringWeights: R Ôćĺ String`

**Actions**:
- `resolve(resolver: R, element: String, context: String)` &rarr; ok | ambiguous | none
- `resolveAll(resolver: R, elements: String, context: String)` &rarr; ok | partial
- `override(resolver: R, element: String, widget: String)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `setWeights(resolver: R, weights: String)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `explain(resolver: R, element: String, context: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound

- `transferred_state: D Ôćĺ String?`
- `reason: D Ôćĺ String`
- `status: D Ôćĺ String`

**Actions**:

- `escalate(source: String, reason: String)` &rarr; ok | no_target
- `getHistory(task_id: String)` &rarr; ok | empty

### AgentMemory [E] <sub>llm-agent</sub>

> Persistent , multi tier memory modeled after cognitive science . Four 
 tiers : working memory ( always in context , like CPU registers ) , episodic 
 ( timestamped interactions , answers what happened? ) , semantic ( facts 
 as embeddings , answers what do I know? ) , procedural ( learned skills , 
 answers how do I do this? ) . The agent actively manages its own memory 
 via tool calls self editing memory , not passive storage .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `entries: Set<E>`
- `memory_type: E Ôćĺ String`
- `content: E Ôćĺ String`
- `embedding: E Ôćĺ List<Float>?`
- `timestamp: E Ôćĺ DateTime`
- `metadata: E Ôćĺ String?`
- `working_memory: List<{ label: String, content: String, max_tokens: Int }>`
- `consolidation_queue: List<String>`

**Actions**:
- `remember(content: String, memory_type: String, metadata: String?)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `recall(query: String, memory_type: String, k: Int)` &rarr; ok | empty
- `editWorkingMemory(label: String, new_content: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `forget(entry: E)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `consolidate()` &rarr; ok | empty
- `search(query: String, filters: { memory_type: String?, after: DateTime?, before: DateTime? }?)` &rarr; ok | empty
- `getWorkingMemory()` &rarr; ok

### Consensus [N] `@gate` <sub>llm-agent</sub>

> Multi agent decision making when agents produce contradictory results 
 or propose incompatible strategies . Supports voting ( simple majority , 
 weighted , unanimous ) , confidence based resolution ( with overconfidence 
 discounting ) , and iterative refinement ( agents debate until convergence ) .

- `outcome: N Ôćĺ { decision: String, method: String, round: Int }?`

**Actions**:
- `create(proposal: String, method: String, max_rounds: Int)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `vote(session: N, agent_id: String, position: String, confidence: Float, reasoning: String)` &rarr; ok | already_voted
- `tally(session: N)` &rarr; ok | deadlock
- `challenge(session: N, agent_id: String, counter_argument: String)` &rarr; ok | max_rounds_exceeded
- `resolve(session: N)` &rarr; ok | unresolvable
- `setWeight(session: N, agent_id: String, weight: Float)` &rarr; ok | notfound

 DesignToken concept with initialization , plugin registry integration , 
 and active theme management . Framework specific UI adapters ( React 
 Context , CompositionLocal , NativeScript globals ) consume this 
 provider for token resolution and theme switching .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `instance: P Ôćĺ String`
- `pluginRef: P Ôćĺ String`
- `status: P Ôćĺ String`
- `activeTheme: P Ôćĺ String`
- `tokenCache: P Ôćĺ String`
- `config: P Ôćĺ String`

**Actions**:
- `initialize(provider: P, config: String)` &rarr; ok | configError
- `resolve(provider: P, tokenName: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `switchTheme(provider: P, theme: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `getTokens(provider: P)` &rarr; ok
- `export(provider: P, format: String)` &rarr; ok | unsupported

### DesktopAdapter [A] <sub>ui-app</sub>

> Translate Navigator transitions , Shell zones , and platform events 
 into desktop specific primitives . Maps destinations to window 
 focus creation , zones to panels and main window regions , overlays 
 to modal dialogs , and keyboard shortcuts ( Cmd [ , Alt Left ) to 
 Navigator actions . Supports multi window management , menubar 
 integration , and system tray interaction .

**State**:
- `outputs: A Ôćĺ String`

**Actions**:
- `normalize(adapter: A, props: String)` &rarr; ok | error

### DevServer [D] `@category(devtools)` <sub>specs</sub>

> Coordinate the local development server lifecycle : start , 
 stop , and query status . File watching is delegated to 
 Resource ( change detection ) , recompilation is triggered by 
 syncs ( Resource changes generation pipeline ) , and output 
 is written through Emitter ( content addressed writes ) .

**State**:
- `sessions: Set<D>`
- `port: D Ôćĺ Int`
- `status: D Ôćĺ String`
- `watchDirs: D Ôćĺ List<String>`

**Actions**:
- `start(port: Int, watchDirs: List<String>)` &rarr; ok | portInUse
- `stop(session: D)` &rarr; ok
- `status(session: D)` &rarr; running | stopped

- `setConstraints(element: E, constraints: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound

**Actions**:

- `addExample(dataset: V, input: String, expected: String, rubric: String?, tags: List<String>)` &rarr; ok | notfound

 ( stdio , SSE , HTTP ) , and hierarchical tool grouping . When 
 @ hierarchical trait is present , generates path based resource 
 URIs and list children get ancestors tool variants . 
 Enrichment content from Projection is passed through for 
 tool description enhancement . 
 See Architecture doc Section 2.5 .

**State**:
- `tools: Set<M>`
- `serverName: M Ôćĺ String`
- `transport: M Ôćĺ String`
- `version: M Ôćĺ String`
- `concept: M Ôćĺ String`
- `action: M Ôćĺ String`
- `mcpType: M Ôćĺ String`
- `toolName: M Ôćĺ String`
- `description: M Ôćĺ String`
- `parentPath: M Ôćĺ String?`
- `childrenTool: M Ôćĺ String?`
- `ancestorsTool: M Ôćĺ String?`
- `content: M Ôćĺ String`

**Actions**:
- `generate(projection: String, config: String)` &rarr; ok | tooManyTools
- `validate(tool: M)` &rarr; ok | missingDescription
- `listTools(concept: String)` &rarr; ok

### ModelRouter [R] <sub>llm-core</sub>

**Actions**:

- `route(task_type: String, complexity: Float?, cost_limit: Float?, latency_limit: Int?)` &rarr; ok | no_route

### PessimisticLock [L] `@gate` <sub>collaboration</sub>

> Prevent conflicts by granting exclusive write access to a resource , 
 serializing edits rather than reconciling them after the fact . 
 Complementary to ConflictResolution use locking for non mergeable 
 content ( binary files , legal documents ) and resolution for mergeable 
 content ( text , structured data ) . checkOut may complete after an 
 arbitrarily long wait if the resource is locked and the requester 
 is queued .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `locks: Set<L>`
- `resource: L Ôćĺ String`
- `holder: L Ôćĺ String`
- `acquired: L Ôćĺ String`
- `expires: L Ôćĺ String?`
- `reason: L Ôćĺ String?`
- `queue: String Ôćĺ List<{ requester: String, requested: String }>`

**Actions**:
- `checkOut(resource: String, holder: String, duration: Int?, reason: String?)` &rarr; ok | alreadyLocked | queued
- `checkIn(lockId: L)` &rarr; ok | notFound | notHolder
- `breakLock(lockId: L, breaker: String, reason: String)` &rarr; ok | notFound | unauthorized
- `renew(lockId: L, additionalDuration: Int)` &rarr; ok | notFound | notHolder
- `queryLocks(resource: String?)` &rarr; ok
- `queryQueue(resource: String)` &rarr; ok

### Signature [G] <sub>llm-prompt</sub>

### StateGraph [H] `@gate` <sub>llm-agent</sub>

> Graph based orchestration with typed state flowing through nodes , 
 conditional edges evaluated by LLMs , first class cycles , durable 
 checkpoints , and time travel . The industry standard for agent workflow 
 orchestration . Fundamentally different from Workflow ( which is an 
 acyclic state machine ) : StateGraph has typed flowing state mutated 
 by each node , LLM evaluated conditional edges , explicit support for 
 cycles , state reducers for concurrent merging , and subgraph nesting .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `graphs: Set<H>`
- `nodes: H Ôćĺ List<{ id: String, type: String, handler: String }>`
- `edges: H Ôćĺ List<{ source: String, target: String, condition: String? }>`
- `state_schema: H Ôćĺ String`
- `entry_point: H Ôćĺ String`
- `finish_points: H Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `execution_state: H Ôćĺ String?`
- `checkpoints: H Ôćĺ List<{ id: String, state: String, timestamp: DateTime, node_id: String }>`
- `reducers: H Ôćĺ List<{ field: String, reducer: String }>`
- `subgraphs: H Ôćĺ List<{ node_id: String, graph_ref: String }>`

**Actions**:
- `create(state_schema: String)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `addNode(graph: H, id: String, type: String, handler: String)` &rarr; ok | duplicate
- `addEdge(graph: H, source: String, target: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `addConditionalEdge(graph: H, source: String, targets: List<{ condition: String, target: String }>)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `setEntryPoint(graph: H, node_id: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `setFinishPoint(graph: H, node_ids: List<String>)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `addReducer(graph: H, field: String, reducer: String)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `addSubgraph(graph: H, node_id: String, subgraph: H)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `compile(graph: H)` &rarr; ok | invalid
- `execute(graph: H, initial_state: String)` &rarr; ok | error | waiting_for_human
- `checkpoint(graph: H)` &rarr; ok | not_executing
- `restore(graph: H, checkpoint_id: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `timeTravel(graph: H, checkpoint_id: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound
- `fork(graph: H, checkpoint_id: String)` &rarr; ok | notfound

 unavailable , local syncs execute on same runtime only .

- `conflicts: List<ActionCompletion>`

**Actions**:

- `onCompletion(completion: ActionCompletion)` &rarr; ok
- `evaluateWhere(bindings: Bindings, queries: List<QueryPlan>)` &rarr; ok | error
- `queueSync(sync: CompiledSync, bindings: Bindings, flow: String)` &rarr; ok

### WinUIAdapter [A] <sub>ui-render</sub>

> Normalize framework neutral props into WinUI 3 specific bindings . 
 Transforms Clef Surface s generic event model into WinUI conventions : 
 XAML control properties , x : Bind data binding , PointerPressed 
 Tapped events , StackPanel Grid layout . Supports Windows 11

 Implementation in C or Rust , runs natively on Windows .

### WorkItem [W] `@gate` <sub>process-human</sub>

> Manage the lifecycle of human tasks : offering to candidate pools , 
 claiming by individuals , completing with form data , delegating , and releasing .

**Capabilities**: persistent-storage

**State**:
- `items: Set<W>`
- `step_ref: W Ôćĺ String`
- `status: W Ôćĺ String`
- `assignee: W Ôćĺ String?`
- `candidate_pool: W Ôćĺ List<String>`
- `form_schema: W Ôćĺ String?`
- `form_data: W Ôćĺ Bytes?`
- `priority: W Ôćĺ Int`
- `due_at: W Ôćĺ DateTime?`
- `claimed_at: W Ôćĺ DateTime?`
- `completed_at: W Ôćĺ DateTime?`

**Actions**:
- `create(step_ref: String, candidate_pool: Bytes, form_schema: String, priority: Int)` &rarr; ok
- `claim(item: W, assignee: String)` &rarr; ok | not_offered | not_authorized
- `start(item: W)` &rarr; ok | not_claimed
- `complete(item: W, form_data: Bytes)` &rarr; ok | not_active | validation_failed
- `reject(item: W, reason: String)` &rarr; ok | not_active
- `delegate(item: W, new_assignee: String)` &rarr; ok | not_claimed
- `release(item: W)` &rarr; ok | not_claimed

### extension
_v0.1.0_ ÔÇö `repertoire/concepts/extension`

> General-purpose extension and plugin support ÔÇö lifecycle management, permissions, configuration, messaging, and contribution points. Host-agnostic coordination layer that routes to host-specific providers (browser, VSCode, Figma, etc.) via discriminator-based syncs. concepts: ExtensionManifest: spec: ./extension-manifest.concept params: M: { as: manifest, description: "Extension manifest declaration" } ExtensionHost: spec: ./extension-host.concept params: H: { as: extension, description: "Installed extension instance" } ContributionPoint: spec: ./contribution-point.concept params: C: { as: contribution-point, description: "Host contribution point" } ExtensionMessaging: spec: ./extension-messaging.concept params: E: { as: channel, description: "Messaging channel" } ExtensionPermission: spec: ./extension-permission.concept params: P: { as: permission, description: "Extension permission" } ExtensionStorage: spec: ./extension-storage.concept params: S: { as: store, description: "Per-extension storage instance" } ExtensionConfig: spec: ./extension-config.concept params: C: { as: config, description: "Per-extension configuration" } syncs: required: - path: ./syncs/required/host-register-on-install.sync description: "Extensions register with PluginRegistry on install" - path: ./syncs/required/permission-check-access.sync description: "Permission checks route through AccessControl for three-valued decisions" - path: ./syncs/required/manifest-validate.sync description: "Manifest registration triggers Validator schema validation" recommended: - path: ./syncs/recommended/config-cache-invalidate.sync description: "Config changes invalidate cached values in Cache" - path: ./syncs/recommended/host-lifecycle-event.sync description: "Lifecycle transitions dispatch events via EventBus" - path: ./syncs/recommended/host-unmount-on-deactivate.sync description: "Extension deactivation unmounts UI via Host" - path: ./syncs/recommended/contribution-widget-register.sync description: "Widget-type contributions route to Widget for rendering" - path: ./syncs/recommended/contribution-nav-register.sync description: "Navigation-type contributions route to Navigator for registration" - ### package
_v0.1.0_ ÔÇö `repertoire/concepts/package`

> Package management ÔÇö dependency resolution, lockfile serialization, artifact fetching, transactional installation, registry indexing, content-addressed storage, feature flags, vulnerability auditing, and publication with provenance attestation. Provides the full dependency lifecycle from manifest authoring through installation and publishing. concepts: # --- Core concepts --- Manifest: spec: ./core/manifest.concept params: P: { as: project, description: "Project manifest" } Resolver: spec: ./core/resolver.concept params: R: { as: resolution, description: "Dependency resolution" } Lockfile: spec: ./core/lockfile.concept params: L: { as: lockfile, description: "Serialized resolution graph" } Registry: spec: ./core/registry.concept params: M: { as: module, description: "Published module record" } FeatureFlag: spec: ./core/feature-flag.concept params: F: { as: flag, description: "Compile-time feature toggle" } ComponentManifest: spec: ./core/component-manifest.concept params: C: { as: component, description: "Module capability manifest" } # --- Distribution concepts --- Fetcher: spec: ./distribution/fetcher.concept params: D: { as: download, description: "Artifact download" } Installer: spec: ./distribution/installer.concept params: I: { as: installation, description: "Installation generation" } ContentStore: spec: ./distribution/content-store.concept params: B: { as: blob, description: "Content-addressed blob" } Publisher: spec: ./distribution/publisher.concept params: U: { as: publication, description: "Publication record" } Auditor: spec: ./distribution/auditor.concept params: A: { as: audit, description: "Vulnerability audit" } Download: spec: ./distribution/download.concept params: D: { as: download, description: "Platform artifact distribution" } SelfUpdate: spec: ./distribution/self-update.concept params: U: { as: update, description: "Binary self-update lifecycle" } syncs: required: - path: ./syncs/required/manifest-to-resolution.sync description: "Validated manifest triggers dependency resolution via Resolver" - path: ./syncs/required/resolution-to-lockfile.sync description: "Successful resolution is persisted as a lockfile" - path: ./syncs/required/lockfile-to-fetch.sync description: "Written lockfile triggers batch artifact download" - path: ./syncs/required/fetch-to-install.sync description: "Fetched artifacts are staged into a new installation generation" - path: ./syncs/required/stage-to-activate.sync description: "Staged installation is atomically activated" - path: ./syncs/required/publish-to-registry.sync description: "Uploaded publication is indexed in the Registry" - path: ./syncs/required/integrity-check-on-fetch.sync description: "Every fetched artifact is verified against the ContentStore" - path: ./syncs/required/feature-unification.sync description: "Feature flags are unified across the dependency graph after resolution" recommended: - path: ./syncs/recommended/auto-audit-on-install.sync description: "Activated installation triggers eventual vulnerability audit" - path: ./syncs/recommended/provenance-on-publish.sync description: "Packaged artifact receives attestation, SBOM, and signature before upload" integration: - path: ./syncs/integration/garbage-collect-on-clean.sync description: "Cleaned installation generations trigger ContentStore garbage collection" widgets: - path: ./widgets/dependency-tree.widget description: "Interactive dependency tree viewer for package manifests" - path: ./widgets/audit-report.widget description: "Security audit report panel with severity breakdown and remediation" - path: ./widgets/registry-search.widget description: "Search interface for the package registry with type-ahead suggestions" surface: entityAffordances: - concept: Manifest detail: dependency-tree - concept: Auditor detail: audit-report - concept: Registry card: registry-search uses: - suite: infrastructure concepts: - name: PluginRegistry - suite: generation concepts: - name: Emitter optional: true

### score-auto

### semantic
